    4601             : nsresult
    4602           0 : QuotaManager::UpgradeStorageFrom1_0To2_0(mozIStorageConnection* aConnection)
    4603             : {
    4604             :   AssertIsOnIOThread();
    4605             :   MOZ_ASSERT(aConnection);
    4606             : 
    4607             :   // The upgrade consists of a number of logically distinct bugs that
    4608             :   // intentionally got fixed at the same time to trigger just one major
    4609             :   // version bump.
    4610             :   //
    4611             :   //
    4612             :   // Morgue directory cleanup
    4613             :   // [Feature/Bug]:
    4614             :   // The original bug that added "on demand" morgue cleanup is 1165119.
    4615             :   //
    4616             :   // [Mutations]:
    4617             :   // Morgue directories are removed from all origin directories during the
    4618             :   // upgrade process. Origin initialization and usage calculation doesn't try
    4619             :   // to remove morgue directories anymore.
    4620             :   //
    4621             :   // [Downgrade-incompatible changes]:
    4622             :   // Morgue directories can reappear if user runs an already upgraded profile
    4623             :   // in an older version of Firefox. Morgue directories then prevent current
    4624             :   // Firefox from initializing and using the storage.
    4625             :   //
    4626             :   //
    4627             :   // App data removal
    4628             :   // [Feature/Bug]:
    4629             :   // The bug that removes isApp flags is 1311057.
    4630             :   //
    4631             :   // [Mutations]:
    4632             :   // Origin directories with appIds are removed during the upgrade process.
    4633             :   //
    4634             :   // [Downgrade-incompatible changes]:
    4635             :   // Origin directories with appIds can reappear if user runs an already
    4636             :   // upgraded profile in an older version of Firefox. Origin directories with
    4637             :   // appIds don't prevent current Firefox from initializing and using the
    4638             :   // storage, but they wouldn't ever be removed again, potentially causing
    4639             :   // problems once appId is removed from origin attributes.
    4640             :   //
    4641             :   //
    4642             :   // Strip obsolete origin attributes
    4643             :   // [Feature/Bug]:
    4644             :   // The bug that strips obsolete origin attributes is 1314361.
    4645             :   //
    4646             :   // [Mutations]:
    4647             :   // Origin directories with obsolete origin attributes are renamed and their
    4648             :   // metadata files are updated during the upgrade process.
    4649             :   //
    4650             :   // [Downgrade-incompatible changes]:
    4651             :   // Origin directories with obsolete origin attributes can reappear if user
    4652             :   // runs an already upgraded profile in an older version of Firefox. Origin
    4653             :   // directories with obsolete origin attributes don't prevent current Firefox
    4654             :   // from initializing and using the storage, but they wouldn't ever be upgraded
    4655             :   // again, potentially causing problems in future.
    4656             :   //
    4657             :   //
    4658             :   // File manager directory renaming (client specific)
    4659             :   // [Feature/Bug]:
    4660             :   // The original bug that added "on demand" file manager directory renaming is
    4661             :   // 1056939.
    4662             :   //
    4663             :   // [Mutations]:
    4664             :   // All file manager directories are renamed to contain the ".files" suffix.
    4665             :   //
    4666             :   // [Downgrade-incompatible changes]:
    4667             :   // File manager directories with the ".files" suffix prevent older versions of
    4668             :   // Firefox from initializing and using the storage.
    4669             :   // File manager directories without the ".files" suffix can appear if user
    4670             :   // runs an already upgraded profile in an older version of Firefox. File
    4671             :   // manager directories without the ".files" suffix then prevent current
    4672             :   // Firefox from initializing and using the storage.
